| <span data-ttu-id="87bf7-1768">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87bf7-1768">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="87bf7-1769">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87bf7-1769">Value</span></span> |
